# Spanish Civil War - Falange Wins
news_event = {
	id = worldstage.12
	title = worldstage.12.t
	desc = worldstage.12.d 
	picture = GFX_news_event_spr_francoist_civil_war_victory

	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	immediate = {
		clr_global_flag = world_stage_theater_spanish_cw_is_active
		set_global_flag = world_stage_theater_spanish_cw_is_over
		set_global_flag = world_stage_theater_spanish_cw_falange_won
		every_state = {
			limit = { OR = { check_variable = { theater_owner_coalition = 8 } check_variable = { theater_owner_coalition = 9 } } }
			set_variable = { theater_owner_coalition = 4 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = worldstage.12.axis
		trigger = {
			has_government = fascism
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = world_stage_spanish_cw_helped_falange }
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_stage_helped_falange_trigger
			add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
				cost_reduction = 0.75
				category = air_doctrine
			}
			add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
				cost_reduction = 0.75
				category = land_doctrine
			}
			add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
				cost_reduction = 0.75
				category = naval_doctrine
			}
			add_war_support = 0.05
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = worldstage.12.komin
		trigger = {
			has_government = communism
		}
		add_war_support = -0.05
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = world_stage_spanish_cw_helped_republica }
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_stage_helped_republica_trigger
			add_war_support = -0.05
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = worldstage.12.other
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = communism
				has_government = fascism
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = world_stage_spanish_cw_helped_falange }
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_stage_helped_falange_trigger
			add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
				cost_reduction = 0.75
				category = air_doctrine
			}
			add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
				cost_reduction = 0.75
				category = land_doctrine
			}
			add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
				cost_reduction = 0.75
				category = naval_doctrine
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = world_stage_spanish_cw_helped_republica }
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_stage_helped_republica_trigger
			add_war_support = -0.05
		}
	}
}

# Spanish Civil War - Repblica Wins
news_event = {
	id = worldstage.13
	title = worldstage.13.t
	desc = worldstage.13.d 
	picture = GFX_news_event_generic_rally2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	immediate = {
		clr_global_flag = world_stage_theater_spanish_cw_is_active
		set_global_flag = world_stage_theater_spanish_cw_is_over
		set_global_flag = world_stage_theater_spanish_cw_republica_won
		every_state = {
			limit = { OR = { check_variable = { theater_owner_coalition = 8 } check_variable = { theater_owner_coalition = 9 } } }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = league_of_nations_exists }
				set_variable = { theater_owner_coalition = 5 }
			} else = { set_variable = { theater_owner_coalition = 4 } }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = worldstage.13.axis
		trigger = {
			has_government = fascism
		}
		add_war_support = -0.05
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = world_stage_spanish_cw_helped_falange }
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_stage_helped_falange_trigger
			add_war_support = -0.05
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = worldstage.13.komin
		trigger = {
			has_government = communism
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = world_stage_spanish_cw_helped_republica }
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_stage_helped_republica_trigger
			add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
				cost_reduction = 0.75
				category = air_doctrine
			}
			add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
				cost_reduction = 0.75
				category = land_doctrine
			}
			add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
				cost_reduction = 0.75
				category = naval_doctrine
			}
			add_war_support = 0.05
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = worldstage.13.other
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = communism
				has_government = fascism
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = world_stage_spanish_cw_helped_republica }
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_stage_helped_republica_trigger
			add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
				cost_reduction = 0.75
				category = air_doctrine
			}
			add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
				cost_reduction = 0.75
				category = land_doctrine
			}
			add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
				cost_reduction = 0.75
				category = naval_doctrine
			}
			add_war_support = 0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = world_stage_spanish_cw_helped_republica }
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_stage_helped_falange_trigger
			add_war_support = -0.05
		}
	}

news_event = {
	id = worldstage.14
	title = worldstage.14.t
	desc = worldstage.14.d 
	picture = GFX_news_event_soviet_tanks

	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes show_major = { NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_worldstage_notification } }
	
	# immediate: none, effect handled by focus
	
	option = {
		name = worldstage.14.axis
		trigger = {
			has_government = fascism
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_scope_republica
			add_to_variable = {
				var = 111.world_stage_power
				value = 5
				tooltip = add_world_stage_power_no_scope_tt
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_to_republica = 1 }
			if = { limit = { 35 = { has_state_flag = theater_is_active } }  subtract_from_temp_variable = { bonus_to_republica = 0.25 } }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
				set_temp_variable = { bonus_to_republica = 1 }
				if = { limit = { 35 = { has_state_flag = theater_is_active } }  subtract_from_temp_variable = { bonus_to_republica = 0.25 } }
			}
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { 35 = { has_state_flag = theater_is_active } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = theater_scope_madrid
				if = {
					limit = { var:world_stage_metropolis = { check_variable = { 35.coalition_side_attack = 8 } } }
					add_to_variable = {
						35.defender_strategic_advantage = bonus_to_republica
						tooltip = world_stage_add_strategic_advantage_attacker
					}

		}

		name = worldstage.17.axis2
		trigger = {
			var:world_stage_metropolis = { check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = 3 } }

		}

	}

	}
}

	picture = GFX_news_ww2_starts_wide

	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes show_major = { NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_worldstage_notification } }
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { global.theater_owner_norway = 1 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = worldstage.45.axis
		trigger = { var:world_stage_metropolis = { check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = 3 } } }
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { tag = REI } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = world_stage_theater_norway_is_active_tt
				custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_name_germany
				add_to_variable = {
					placeholder_var = 60
					tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_norway
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					placeholder_var = 30
					tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_norway
				}
			}

# NOTE: the follwoing 4 events are for when PRT/HIR join a coalition while the 2nd world war is ongoing, either through focuses or joining AXS/ALY/COM's faction

# Netherlands Joins War: Allies! Open New Front!
news_event = {
	id = worldstage.841
	title = worldstage.841.t
	desc = worldstage.841.d 
	picture = GFX_news_ww2_starts_wide

	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	immediate = {
		107 = { set_state_flag = worldstage_AI_active } # netherlands # awake the AI
		if = {
			limit = { 8 = { check_variable = { theater_owner_coalition = 3 } } }	# priority is taking France
			8 = {
				set_state_flag = theater_is_active
				add_to_variable = { world_stage_power_deployed_by^107 = 5 }	
				107 = { add_to_variable = { world_stage_power = -5 } }
				add_to_variable = { world_stage_power_deployed_by^var:theater_owner = 1 }
				var:theater_owner = { add_to_variable = { world_stage_power = -1 } }
				set_variable = { coalition_side_attack = 1 }	# Allies
				world_stage_state_update_current_day = yes 
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { 6 = { check_variable = { theater_owner_coalition = 3 } } }
			6 = {
				set_state_flag = theater_is_active
				add_to_variable = { world_stage_power_deployed_by^107 = 5 }	
				107 = { add_to_variable = { world_stage_power = -5 } }
				add_to_variable = { world_stage_power_deployed_by^var:theater_owner = 1 }
				var:theater_owner = { add_to_variable = { world_stage_power = -1 } }
				set_variable = { coalition_side_attack = 1 }	# Allies
				world_stage_state_update_current_day = yes 
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = { tag = HIR }
		name = worldstage.84.self
		custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_scope_netherlands
		custom_effect_tooltip = join_coalition_allies
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = HIR } check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = 1 } }
		name = worldstage.84.good
		custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_scope_netherlands
		custom_effect_tooltip = join_coalition_allies
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = HIR } check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = 3 } }
		name = worldstage.84.bad
		custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_scope_netherlands
		custom_effect_tooltip = join_coalition_allies
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = HIR check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = 1 } check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = 3 } } }
		name = worldstage.84.neutral
		custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_scope_netherlands
		custom_effect_tooltip = join_coalition_allies
	}
}

# Netherlands Joins War: Allies! No New Front

# Netherlands Joins War: Axis! Open New Front!
news_event = {
	id = worldstage.845
	title = worldstage.845.t
	desc = worldstage.845.d 
	picture = GFX_news_ww2_starts_wide

	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	immediate = {
		107 = { set_state_flag = worldstage_AI_active } # netherlands # awake the AI
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = world_stage_world_war_2_is_active 8 = { check_variable = { theater_owner_coalition = 1 } } }	# priority is taking France
			8 = {
				set_state_flag = theater_is_active
				add_to_variable = { world_stage_power_deployed_by^107 = 5 }	
				107 = { add_to_variable = { world_stage_power = -5 } }
				add_to_variable = { world_stage_power_deployed_by^var:theater_owner = 1 }
				var:theater_owner = { add_to_variable = { world_stage_power = -1 } }
				set_variable = { coalition_side_attack = 3 }	# Axis
				world_stage_state_update_current_day = yes 
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = world_stage_world_war_3_is_active 8 = { check_variable = { theater_owner_coalition = 2 } } }
			8 = {
				set_state_flag = theater_is_active
				add_to_variable = { world_stage_power_deployed_by^107 = 5 }	
				107 = { add_to_variable = { world_stage_power = -5 } }
				add_to_variable = { world_stage_power_deployed_by^var:theater_owner = 1 }
				var:theater_owner = { add_to_variable = { world_stage_power = -1 } }
				set_variable = { coalition_side_attack = 3 }	# Axis
				world_stage_state_update_current_day = yes 
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = world_stage_world_war_2_is_active 6 = { check_variable = { theater_owner_coalition = 1 } } }
			6 = {
				set_state_flag = theater_is_active
				add_to_variable = { world_stage_power_deployed_by^107 = 5 }	
				107 = { add_to_variable = { world_stage_power = -5 } }
				add_to_variable = { world_stage_power_deployed_by^var:theater_owner = 1 }
				var:theater_owner = { add_to_variable = { world_stage_power = -1 } }
				set_variable = { coalition_side_attack = 3 }	# Axis
				world_stage_state_update_current_day = yes 
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = world_stage_world_war_3_is_active 6 = { check_variable = { theater_owner_coalition = 2 } } }
			6 = {
				set_state_flag = theater_is_active
				add_to_variable = { world_stage_power_deployed_by^107 = 5 }	
				107 = { add_to_variable = { world_stage_power = -5 } }
				add_to_variable = { world_stage_power_deployed_by^var:theater_owner = 1 }
				var:theater_owner = { add_to_variable = { world_stage_power = -1 } }
				set_variable = { coalition_side_attack = 3 }	# Axis
				world_stage_state_update_current_day = yes 
			}
		}	# NOTE: this check is more complex since there are multiple paths and multiple possible enemies
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = { tag = HIR }
		name = worldstage.84.self
		custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_scope_netherlands
		custom_effect_tooltip = join_coalition_axis
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = HIR } check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = 3 } }
		name = worldstage.84.good
		custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_scope_netherlands
		custom_effect_tooltip = join_coalition_axis
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = HIR }
			OR = {
				AND = { check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = 1 } has_global_flag = world_stage_world_war_2_is_active }
				AND = { check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = 2 } has_global_flag = world_stage_world_war_3_is_active }
			}
		}
		name = worldstage.84.bad
		custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_scope_netherlands
		custom_effect_tooltip = join_coalition_axis
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = HIR }
			if = { limit = { has_global_flag = world_stage_world_war_2_is_active } NOT = { check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = 1 } } }
			if = { limit = { has_global_flag = world_stage_world_war_3_is_active } NOT = { check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = 2 } } }
		}
		name = worldstage.84.neutral
		custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_scope_netherlands
		custom_effect_tooltip = join_coalition_axis
	}
}

			add_to_variable = { world_stage_power_deployed_by^var:theater_owner = 1 }
			var:theater_owner = { add_to_variable = { world_stage_power = -1 } }
			set_variable = { coalition_side_attack = 2 }	# Commintern
			world_stage_state_update_current_day = yes 
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = { tag = PRT }
		name = worldstage.85.self
		custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_scope_portugal
		custom_effect_tooltip = join_coalition_commintern
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = PRT } check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = 1 } }
		name = worldstage.85.good
		custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_scope_portugal
		custom_effect_tooltip = join_coalition_commintern
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = PRT } check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = 3 } }
		name = worldstage.85.bad
		custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_scope_portugal
		custom_effect_tooltip = join_coalition_commintern
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = PRT check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = 1 } check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = 3 } } }
		name = worldstage.85.neutral
		custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_scope_portugal
		custom_effect_tooltip = join_coalition_commintern
	}
}

# Portugal Joins War: Cominter! No New Front
news_event = {
	id = worldstage.854
	title = worldstage.854.t
	desc = worldstage.854.d 
	picture = GFX_news_ww2_starts_wide

	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	immediate = { 108 = { set_state_flag = worldstage_AI_active }	} # portugal # awake the AI
	
	option = {
		trigger = { tag = PRT }
		name = worldstage.86.self
		custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_scope_portugal
		custom_effect_tooltip = join_coalition_commintern
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = PRT } check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = global.coalition_portugal } }
		name = worldstage.86.good
		custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_scope_portugal
		custom_effect_tooltip = join_coalition_commintern
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = PRT } check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = global.coalition_portugal_enemy } }
		name = worldstage.86.bad
		custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_scope_portugal
		custom_effect_tooltip = join_coalition_commintern
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = PRT check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = global.coalition_portugal } check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = global.coalition_portugal_enemy } } }
		name = worldstage.86.neutral
		custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_scope_portugal
		custom_effect_tooltip = join_coalition_commintern
	}
}

# Portugal Joins War: Axis! Open New Front! (this only triggers if Spain is an active enemy)
news_event = {
	id = worldstage.855
	title = worldstage.855.t
	desc = worldstage.855.d 
	picture = GFX_news_ww2_starts_wide

	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	immediate = {
		108 = { set_state_flag = worldstage_AI_active } # portugal # awake the AI
		35 = {
			set_state_flag = theater_is_active
			add_to_variable = { world_stage_power_deployed_by^108 = 5 }	
			108 = { add_to_variable = { world_stage_power = -5 } }
			add_to_variable = { world_stage_power_deployed_by^var:theater_owner = 1 }
			var:theater_owner = { add_to_variable = { world_stage_power = -1 } }
			set_variable = { coalition_side_attack = 3 }	# Axis
			world_stage_state_update_current_day = yes 
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = { tag = PRT }
		name = worldstage.85.self
		custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_scope_portugal
		custom_effect_tooltip = join_coalition_axis
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = PRT } check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = 3 } }
		name = worldstage.85.good
		custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_scope_portugal
		custom_effect_tooltip = join_coalition_axis
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = PRT }
			OR = {
				AND = { check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = 1 } has_global_flag = world_stage_world_war_2_is_active }
				AND = { check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = 2 } has_global_flag = world_stage_world_war_3_is_active }
			}
		}
		name = worldstage.85.bad
		custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_scope_portugal
		custom_effect_tooltip = join_coalition_axis
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = PRT }
			if = { limit = { has_global_flag = world_stage_world_war_2_is_active } NOT = { check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = 1 } } }
			if = { limit = { has_global_flag = world_stage_world_war_3_is_active } NOT = { check_variable = { world_stage_coalition = 2 } } }
		}
		name = worldstage.85.neutral
		custom_effect_tooltip = metropolis_scope_portugal
		custom_effect_tooltip = join_coalition_axis
	}
}

# Portugal Joins War: Axis! No New Front
